, &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">A stands for automatic. <i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\">( avtomat</i> )<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-size: large;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; (<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"> Kalashnikova </i>)<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-size: large;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">47 stands for the year off build.<o:p></o:p></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><br /></span></span>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<iframe width=\"320\" height=\"266\" class=\"YOUTUBE-iframe-video\" data-thumbnail-src=\"https://i.ytimg.com/vi/Y4BeJ-64294/0.jpg\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/Y4BeJ-64294?feature=player_embedded\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen></iframe></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In 2004 Vladmir Putin sent George W Bush some Russian Vodka in a bottle shaped like a AK-47, just to remind him of its popularity in USA.. what with its reliable firing rate of 700 round per minute. It was also to remind that that AK-47 is an invention of Russia and not Hollywood.&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">An AK-47 requires NIL training. Just load , shoot and kill. There is a selector switch for single shot of full automatic fire. It has passed every torture test of getting buried in ice or sand or dirty salt water, thrown down cliffs and very time the gun fired. It created large exit wounds and can pass through a car door at 100 metres easily.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">In the Hollywood movie First Blood II, Rambo takes on the entire Viet Cong with a old and battered AK-47.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>His American colleague with a M16 asks him \u201c A beat to shit AK?. Every 12 year old in Nam got that!\u201d <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Rambo looks mighty pleased and gives his trademark<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>laborious side way drawl \u201c Exactly!\u201d </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-GwoSQFq9Ryk/ToDBNowiFoI/AAAAAAAAGiU/s9618z7eUKI/s1600/VBN.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"351\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-GwoSQFq9Ryk/ToDBNowiFoI/AAAAAAAAGiU/s9618z7eUKI/s400/VBN.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">American Marines in Viet Nam were given M16 guns which jammed even in light rain. And they had to face the awesome firepower of the Viet Cong 40 kg warriors whose guns never jammed even if it was covered in heavy mud. So after killing them<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>the Americans used to steal their AK-47 rifles and bullets.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">When your life is on the line you need a reliable weapon, NOT a fancy one on paper. Their bullshit Colt Armalite M16 guns had to be cleaned every 30 rounds, if it had to be reliable. The GIs\u2019 were NOT even issued with rifle cleaning kits. The US military came up with a white washing statement later that the soldiers were given the wrong cartridges\u2014so many lives lost, by the big bull of M16 being maintenance free! </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">If you hold a AK47 and shake it, it rattles . But such a shake given to a M16, does NOT rattle\u2014for the simple reason enough clearances for temperature variations and grit in the system was ignored. So though the AK47 was less accurate in distances greater than 300 metres, they were much more reliable, as the gun never jammed in the thick of battle, at the most inopportune and critical moment. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Most firefights happen within 300 metres range. The maker Kalashnikov was so cock sure that his gun wont jam, that he never bothered to fit them with bayonets..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-KdDHAUGDfPA/ToDCIGe9zXI/AAAAAAAAGjA/cT1Kdp8KDvs/s1600/300px-Rifle_AK_MON.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"221\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-KdDHAUGDfPA/ToDCIGe9zXI/AAAAAAAAGjA/cT1Kdp8KDvs/s640/300px-Rifle_AK_MON.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Just about 4 months after the World trade centre came down in New York, my ship loaded a full shipload of Siberian USED railway tracks at St Petersberg Russia.&nbsp; Siberian railway tracks have the best steel on this planet. &nbsp;I made sure I examined what went into my ships holds. There was NOT a single USED railway track\u2014all were BRAND NEW. It is easy to find a used track, as the bolts and nuts will leave circular marks. Some gigantic Russian mafia export to US government&nbsp;, to be melted in the furnace for military needs.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">One of the reasons Russian AK-47 assault rifle and its later models has stood the test of time , is due to superior metallurgy. Many countries make their own AK-47 guns without licence. Their guns cannot fire 700 rounds a minute and will jam as the metal expands. While the Russian AK-47 will work from minus 40 deg C of Siberia to plus 60 deg centigrade of Kuwait desert.</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Pz14Bmnn3fM/ToDCE7Oe4kI/AAAAAAAAGi8/l8D8b_bajCU/s1600/NK.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"216\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Pz14Bmnn3fM/ToDCE7Oe4kI/AAAAAAAAGi8/l8D8b_bajCU/s640/NK.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">On my last ship I had my Filipino Bosun, who was kidnapped by the Nigerian rebels at Lagos , along with the 2<sup>nd</sup> Mate and the Russian Chief Engineer. He tells me that he used to cry every day, for the couple of months he was with them in the jungles. Then he said that the Russian Chief Engineer was very happy. It seems the rebels used to give him hundreds of AK-47 rifles to overhaul, and in return they used to feed him well with fresh lamb and as many girls as he wanted at night. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">One of my ex- Russian Chief Engineers had told me that at school they were trained to dismantle and assemble AK-47 rifles with eyes blindfolded. It was part of the school curriculum in the cold war era. I remember him telling they there are only 8 parts, and even a retard can do it, it was no big deal.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-JS_-OWFqsno/ToDBg9WlnqI/AAAAAAAAGik/BSj9FQ4dQAw/s1600/DTY.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"440\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-JS_-OWFqsno/ToDBg9WlnqI/AAAAAAAAGik/BSj9FQ4dQAw/s640/DTY.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The AK-47 is a GAS BLOW BACK operated weapon. When the gun if fired and the round detonated the<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>gas of the explosion behind the bullet goes up the barrel, and enters a small port at the top of the barrel near the muzzle, from where it directed to push the working piston mechanism back at the breech. This ejects the spent cartridge and loads a new cartridge, from the magazine to repeat the cycle. The gun reloads by itself.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; s</span>imultaneously the hammer is cocked , and it does it 11 times a second under the automatic fire mode..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Lt Gen Mikael Timofeyevich Klashnikov started his career as a gun designer after getting shot on his shoulder with a nazi shell shrapnel during the Battle of Bryansk in Oct 1941 as a tank commander. </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-yVLJbwEGgiQ/ToDBafH3w7I/AAAAAAAAGig/l_s3y-pehKk/s1600/jnl.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-yVLJbwEGgiQ/ToDBafH3w7I/AAAAAAAAGig/l_s3y-pehKk/s640/jnl.jpg\" width=\"457\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">While in the hospital for 6 long months, he heard soldiers complaining about their guns\u2014which they could NOT officially. , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Chinese loved to trade with Calicut kings as they were very honest and principled. They loved and honoured<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Bodhi Dharma who was a great Kalari sword and martial arts warrior and also a Buddhist saint. </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-IcU_xlF28K8/TnsO0g8hFwI/AAAAAAAAGVc/Azu6cWx-lCI/s1600/Zheng-He-7th-expedition-map_svg.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"484\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-IcU_xlF28K8/TnsO0g8hFwI/AAAAAAAAGVc/Azu6cWx-lCI/s640/Zheng-He-7th-expedition-map_svg.png\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Never mind what Chinese historians or Western historians say, our records state that the Shaolin temple monks were trained in combat by Bodhi Dharma . He taught them the secret Kalari 108 marmas or vulnerable points , which was given to Kerala by Lord Parashurama in 4200 BC. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>This Chinese martial art strain is now called Kungfu<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Calicut kings were honourable and generous men. , They took pride in never breaking their word , once given. So there was NO need for extensive written marine charter party contracts and on the spot cash payments. </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-VmH0Swq9mNY/TqBIQOOc7XI/AAAAAAAAHMQ/Q2qKrfQbLIw/s1600/imagesCAG0IO3L.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-VmH0Swq9mNY/TqBIQOOc7XI/AAAAAAAAHMQ/Q2qKrfQbLIw/s1600/imagesCAG0IO3L.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Sometimes it would be paid in the next voyage, such was the mutual trust. Deals and negotiations were done by clasping each others hands under a white Veshti , and using finger pressure. So though the deal was witnessed by all and concluded, NO body knew the first and last bids and the process. Profit or loss a deal was a deal, and the King would die rather than cheat. Chinese never cheated or stole.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-DVJ9IayoWuU/TntcA0a3CjI/AAAAAAAAGXY/tVoka07nO4A/s1600/imagesmfi.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"248\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-DVJ9IayoWuU/TntcA0a3CjI/AAAAAAAAGXY/tVoka07nO4A/s320/imagesmfi.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\nCompare this with what Portuguese Vasco Da Gama did in 1498.&nbsp; He landed at Kappad beach at Calicut . <br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-kybxSKt5ABY/TntcScg1RbI/AAAAAAAAGXg/6lfZA97u5uI/s1600/imagesnm.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"219\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-kybxSKt5ABY/TntcScg1RbI/AAAAAAAAGXg/6lfZA97u5uI/s320/imagesnm.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nMajority of his&nbsp;sailors had Pirangi Punnu on the penis ( foreign sore ) - and they used to walk with legs apart. <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-wgM7AfCOSj8/TntcI6Dj5aI/AAAAAAAAGXc/lebqmnUAtJE/s1600/ndw.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-wgM7AfCOSj8/TntcI6Dj5aI/AAAAAAAAGXc/lebqmnUAtJE/s400/ndw.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThe Calicut Kings Vaidyar , told the king it is a veneral disease NOT found in Kerala . <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Rpe6qc7FOAo/TnzsX0ha3EI/AAAAAAAAGb4/inme1LoDscc/s1600/imagesCAR8HV8F.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Rpe6qc7FOAo/TnzsX0ha3EI/AAAAAAAAGb4/inme1LoDscc/s1600/imagesCAR8HV8F.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nVasco da Gama has the gall to appraoch the King in his palace and say say that he wants to leave behind four of his white sailors&nbsp;as \"hostages\". <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-rS4m9j_eOrA/Tns6Vjvd0tI/AAAAAAAAGXM/xTkQLJkgfvE/s1600/images+%252818%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-rS4m9j_eOrA/Tns6Vjvd0tI/AAAAAAAAGXM/xTkQLJkgfvE/s1600/images+%252818%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nAs it is the locals women were pissed off by the ugly lecherous behavior and constant ogling of the white sailors. They thought cultured Kerala Hindu women could be had for sex, the way they took the ugly black women in Malindi Kenya , dime a dozen.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-x0FbSR4tUtM/Tns6gT2yVwI/AAAAAAAAGXQ/4TYGYBr0bhs/s1600/images+%252817%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-x0FbSR4tUtM/Tns6gT2yVwI/AAAAAAAAGXQ/4TYGYBr0bhs/s1600/images+%252817%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThe king demanded&nbsp;why?.&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\nGama says \"You also have to give four of your blood relatives as hostages, who has to stay on my ship. This is to make sure promises are kept on both sides.!\" <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-BKPcB6-X-QA/TntgH8QCzAI/AAAAAAAAGYA/uGU0ZPkr7v8/s1600/downloadber.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"310\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-BKPcB6-X-QA/TntgH8QCzAI/AAAAAAAAGYA/uGU0ZPkr7v8/s400/downloadber.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThe king was aghast, at this \"Mexican stand off\" type lack of culture.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-QSkRIFkbfRw/Tns6oshJb9I/AAAAAAAAGXU/yj4QEGZJGP4/s1600/images+%252822%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-QSkRIFkbfRw/Tns6oshJb9I/AAAAAAAAGXU/yj4QEGZJGP4/s1600/images+%252822%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nAt night Vasco da Gama's sailors stole pepper vines in large quantities , literally vanadalising large tracts of pepper groves.&nbsp;( cutting the&nbsp;roots of&nbsp;hundreds of metres long&nbsp;pepper vines)&nbsp;, and took it in pots on their ships in great secrecy. <br />\n<br />\nThey had zilch idea that every inch of their thieving progress was being monitored by dozens of eyes in the dark. When Zamorin was told about this , instead of getting angry, he had a hearty laugh and said \" Vasco Da Gama&nbsp;can steal our pepper plants, and our soil--&nbsp;but&nbsp;there is no way he can steal our Thiruvatira Jnattuvela ( tropical wet weather ).\"<br />\n<br />\nAnd finally that was what thief Vasco Da Gama did. He sailed away taking 4 of Calicut kings blood relatives as hostages to Cochin, without paying customs duty. His goods from Portugal was pathetic-- trinkets, coloured glass, and glass beads for cultured people wearing diamonds, gold and silk.. <br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><em><span style=\"color: black;\">Glass HA-- wrong number !&nbsp; Ancient Indian Vimanas as per Vimanaka Shastra of 5000 BC had heat resistant sodalime glass containers to hold mercury . Our Mahabharata wax palace of 4000 BC, where Draupadi made fun of Duryodhana , had transparent glass windows. The Univeristy of Taxila of 3000 BC had a text Vedic text Shatapata Brahmana . This university had <span style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">10500 seats for world students were available as long as they were more than the age of 16. Students came from as far as Mesopotamia, Greece, Syria, Arabia , Russia, Thailand and China. Our ancient kings placed water filled globe glasses to magnify written texts.</span></span></em></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-lLybmSTZ6FY/TnsPDj1bacI/AAAAAAAAGVk/TpvnDkyGz-8/s1600/columbus+santa+marta.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"246\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-lLybmSTZ6FY/TnsPDj1bacI/AAAAAAAAGVk/TpvnDkyGz-8/s400/columbus+santa+marta.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nAbove is a comparison of Zheng's ship with Columbus's ship Santa Marta.<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">The Kings accountants never needed abacus for complicated accounts calculations.&nbsp; Zheng always wondered at the great mental Mathematical prowess of the Malayalis. By the time the Chinese acoountants finished rat-a-tat, even the King was ready with the answer done in his mind, using Vedic Mathematics&nbsp;. Calicut kings shared their navigation secrets through the treacherous reef bounded Red sea . Or else you have to berth your slow and clumsy Junk at&nbsp;Aden or Salalah and then take a land camel caravan to Mecca. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-PU1x96jc-l8/TnsPPaykZ3I/AAAAAAAAGVo/TBW1NcppILE/s1600/download+%25283%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"429\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-PU1x96jc-l8/TnsPPaykZ3I/AAAAAAAAGVo/TBW1NcppILE/s640/download+%25283%2529.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">The Calicut king was kind to the Chinese and would treat them to lavish spicy dinners and classical music sessions. The Chief of the Chinese junk fleet would always be given a KASAVU PUDAVA , which is a gorgeous multicoloured silk garment with gold threadings . </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-euljDeLo-UQ/Tnt_i5Lgg2I/AAAAAAAAGYs/ahXk8DG_6AU/s1600/nnn.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"200\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-euljDeLo-UQ/Tnt_i5Lgg2I/AAAAAAAAGYs/ahXk8DG_6AU/s200/nnn.png\" width=\"148\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-PbOhRr453Sc/TnuA4Pach1I/AAAAAAAAGYw/82AFLqyVlCg/s1600/mku.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-PbOhRr453Sc/TnuA4Pach1I/AAAAAAAAGYw/82AFLqyVlCg/s1600/mku.png\" width=\"252\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">They also send Kerala Ayurvedic herbs and tonics like Chyawanprash and Ashwagandha , Sandalwood ,Sarasaparilla sherbet cordial, and incense --which the Chinese kings back home loved.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-T3QC4079G5g/TnsPU3733ZI/AAAAAAAAGVs/u2J6l7OiBTA/s1600/images+%25287%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"262\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-T3QC4079G5g/TnsPU3733ZI/AAAAAAAAGVs/u2J6l7OiBTA/s1600/images+%25287%2529.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">There was a time in Sri Lanka when the Sinhalese king who had usurped the throne from a Malayali/Tamil king was literally humiliated by Chinese admiral Zheng He.&nbsp; He drew out the Sinhala soldiers protecting the snooty king by using a decoy force. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Zheng&nbsp;then&nbsp;invaded the palace and captured the arrogant Sinhala king. &nbsp;He took him as a prisoner to&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 18px;\">Quanzhou&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">China, to give the uncultured Sinhala king few \u201clessons in humility\u201d.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">He also took away the tooth of Buddha , which was returned by Chou En Lai in 1960.</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-8jRhmJaSZz4/TnsPal6em_I/AAAAAAAAGVw/hHfLDa5aNkI/s1600/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-8jRhmJaSZz4/TnsPal6em_I/AAAAAAAAGVw/hHfLDa5aNkI/s320/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" width=\"309\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">The rightful Kerala king was re-installed on the throne , and the Sinhala king was sent back as an ordinary citizen . At the same time it is on record that Admiral Zheng , though he was a Muslim eunuch ( got castrated at a young age when he was a prisoner ) was NOT anti-Buddhist.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">During Zheng\u2019s time Calicut was the richest port on this planet. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>India as a whole held 35% of global GDP.&nbsp; Vijayanagara served this port as hinterland.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Admiral Zheng had several record keepers sailing with him on his passages to Calicut. Some of these records are NOT exacly correct. He records Calicut King as a Hindu Brahmin. Well our Calicut kings ( my hometown ) are Kshatriya clan Varmas . They have never belonged to the Kerala Brahmin Namboodiri or Bhattatiri clan . </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Also Zheng\u2019s erroneous <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>records say that Calicut King\u2019s Chiefs were Muslim. Sorry, all his Chief\u2019s were Hindus except Navy<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Marakkars. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">But certain records like\nthe throne peacefully transits to to the King\u2019s sister\u2019s son---that Calicut\ncoins were 60% ,gold and balance silver ---that Calicut silk master weavers were\nvery good in colourful dyeing \u2013 that Calicut people eat no wheat --- that\nZamorin\u2019s had a customs department to collect duty -- that Calicut swords were\nof excellent quality steel-- that Kerala women wore gold bangles, neck chains\nand toe rings-- that in 1407 Admiral Zheng erected a ceremonial stone tablet in\nCheenakotta&nbsp; \u2013that Calicut king and\nCochin king did NOT see eye to eye-- that Kerala people were a martial race\n--that Bodhi Dharma who taught Chinese Kungfu was a Kalari warrior saint from Calicut.etc--\nwas correct</span></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">.</span></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://0.gvt0.com/vi/sbWuk5AjHhg/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/sbWuk5AjHhg&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/sbWuk5AjHhg&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://0.gvt0.com/vi/H2li5qd3k_Q/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/H2li5qd3k_Q&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/H2li5qd3k_Q&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\nZheng noted that unlike in other cultures where son kills father, father kills son, brothers gouge each others eyes -- the succession process in Calicut was a very honourable one.</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">This ceremonial stone also was destroyed along with the dargah at Cheenakotta in Calicut by the British. Wonder what is the need to do all this disservice , to such a famous man. Was it because he was a Mongol Muslim?&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">By the way Zheng He is just a ceremonial name given to Ma He by the Ming emperor in 1403. Calicut people called him Hajiar Shamsuddin. His great grandfather was called Hajiar Bayen.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">There used to be a Jew quarters ( Joota angadi ) and Chinese quarters ( Cheenakotta ) at Calicut. They have all been destroyed and build over by new buildings, with the sub-division and fragmentation Hindu policy of ancestral lands. Zheng He dies in Calicut. </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">On his last voyage he sort of gave unofficial \u201cFrench leave \u201c to some of his Chinese Buddhist men, who went to Mecca in a couple of ships , led by Calicut king's ship-- and came back as Muslims. The ship landed at Aden and his crew went by Caravan-and it too too long for them to come back.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-syji5O0oGg0/TnsXBA0iqFI/AAAAAAAAGW4/_hOrY6RWAGI/s1600/imagesCA092F8K.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"151\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-syji5O0oGg0/TnsXBA0iqFI/AAAAAAAAGW4/_hOrY6RWAGI/s1600/imagesCA092F8K.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">By this time Zheng was a bit power drunk and was not a hand-kisser&nbsp;of the&nbsp;Chinese King. This religious trip to Mecca report was NOT taken well in China by the Confucious sect intellectuals , who were aghast that Zheng tried to mix King\u2019s trade, and religion. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-iSSzAicxd2c/TqBI0cSoPzI/AAAAAAAAHMg/tRBOsHnkSss/s1600/imagesCAZ7KEP9.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"275\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-iSSzAicxd2c/TqBI0cSoPzI/AAAAAAAAHMg/tRBOsHnkSss/s1600/imagesCAZ7KEP9.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<em><span style=\"color: red;\">Above --Calicut king's shipyard at Beypore , Calicut</span></em><br />\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: large; line-height: 115%;\">Zheng was NOT alive to defend himself and lot of false stories were circulated by jealous Confucious followers.</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-1hiKuj6h1zQ/TntetQof1dI/AAAAAAAAGX4/bEEGYZmt3T8/s1600/images+%252812%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-1hiKuj6h1zQ/TntetQof1dI/AAAAAAAAGX4/bEEGYZmt3T8/s1600/images+%252812%2529.jpg\" width=\"310\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">During this time in Calicut , where he stayed at Zamorins guest , he dies a natural death and his body was buried with Muslim honours at Calicut. Haji Shamsuddin\u2019s ( Zheng He\u2019s Muslim name ) dargah existed for 200 years, till the British razed it.</span><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Mysore Muslim invaded king Hyder Ali blew up the Zamorin\u2019s palace, after stealing all the gold from underground vaults . Or the artifacts of Zheng&nbsp;could have been seen by all even today. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-NWpq5B1M9Ak/TntepkjgO8I/AAAAAAAAGX0/Aea3MTwuvAk/s1600/imagesbdr.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-NWpq5B1M9Ak/TntepkjgO8I/AAAAAAAAGX0/Aea3MTwuvAk/s1600/imagesbdr.jpg\" width=\"266\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">The Greatest Admiral of this planet, <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Zheng He was literally erased from history too. The next dynasty after the Ming Dynastry for some strange reason , erased Zheng He\u2019s AMAZING achievements of being the BEST and most respected ambassador China has ever produced.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-G9Csh8Hc7X8/TnsOUrhdatI/AAAAAAAAGVI/ADnpZf5bsZ4/s1600/download+%25282%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"268\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-G9Csh8Hc7X8/TnsOUrhdatI/AAAAAAAAGVI/ADnpZf5bsZ4/s1600/download+%25282%2529.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">When he first came to Calicut on the FIRST voyage with a fleet of more than 300 ships holding more than 31000 Chinese men in 1406, the Calicut locals could NOT even see the horizon and naturally people were very worried. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-BP5JBmY5JzU/TnsQSfYE8QI/AAAAAAAAGWM/gpJSdQIQnns/s1600/columbus+santa+marta.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"246\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-BP5JBmY5JzU/TnsQSfYE8QI/AAAAAAAAGWM/gpJSdQIQnns/s400/columbus+santa+marta.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Dn5ovo-gWD8/TnsRa1ykD3I/AAAAAAAAGWc/3WbSIeG5OTA/s1600/warriors.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"362\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Dn5ovo-gWD8/TnsRa1ykD3I/AAAAAAAAGWc/3WbSIeG5OTA/s1600/warriors.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">It was a terribly ominous scene, with women crying out of fear.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ja8p-TEBRcg/TnteMBmMrqI/AAAAAAAAGXo/VWLBRNBYnOc/s1600/imagesmlp.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"271\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ja8p-TEBRcg/TnteMBmMrqI/AAAAAAAAGXo/VWLBRNBYnOc/s1600/imagesmlp.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Such fear was unwarranted&nbsp;as the deadly Kerala Kalari sword fighters in long and swift snake boats ( holding 100 warriors each ) could have set the not so maneuverable&nbsp;and &nbsp;slow junkss ( max speed 4 knots ) on fire. The huge&nbsp;plaited bamboo reed sails, presented a vulnerable target , with thin but heavy, rose wood FIRE arrows -- any time they wanted-- easy pickings. Yes 300 junks came in , none would go back.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-xuaHQgy5fi0/TnsY8YhR2JI/AAAAAAAAGXI/Uj13_7vleJQ/s1600/images%252B%25252818%252529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"274\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-xuaHQgy5fi0/TnsY8YhR2JI/AAAAAAAAGXI/Uj13_7vleJQ/s1600/images%252B%25252818%252529.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-58_1BXh3R7g/TnsRSkOu4pI/AAAAAAAAGWY/mZVnAU3osTA/s1600/snake%252Bboats.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"241\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-58_1BXh3R7g/TnsRSkOu4pI/AAAAAAAAGWY/mZVnAU3osTA/s1600/snake%252Bboats.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-4bD3XCwOtcg/TnsRoeXKKyI/AAAAAAAAGWg/_se6f8IrCMs/s1600/images+%252813%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"285\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-4bD3XCwOtcg/TnsRoeXKKyI/AAAAAAAAGWg/_se6f8IrCMs/s1600/images+%252813%2529.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">King Zamorin knew that a large fleet was coming as his envoy Narayanan Nair <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>had presented the Chinese king with a most exquisite gold braided cloth, encrusted in diamonds and pearls for his Royal regalia, along with huge ivory tusks , and asked him to increase the trade \u2013and had got a positive reply by carrier pigeon. </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-t1mT-qXv-kE/TnsQJasuELI/AAAAAAAAGWI/Xxed-Q9V0mk/s1600/images+%252816%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"237\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-t1mT-qXv-kE/TnsQJasuELI/AAAAAAAAGWI/Xxed-Q9V0mk/s1600/images+%252816%2529.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">But Admiral Zheng\u2019s personal ship was 600 feet long and this majestic warrior measured seven Chinese feet which is about 6 feet 7 inches of British feet. Three generations of Zheng He\u2019s ancestral fathers honourable dealing with Zamorin was NOT lost on him, <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>and he gave full respect to the people of Calicut. </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-gtWRQIfm1Xo/TnsRNL2T4jI/AAAAAAAAGWU/Dv02_hJjWcY/s1600/images%252B%25252866%252529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-gtWRQIfm1Xo/TnsRNL2T4jI/AAAAAAAAGWU/Dv02_hJjWcY/s1600/images%252B%25252866%252529.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Zheng He\u2019s grandfather was a Haji and he went to Mecca the first time in Calicut Kings\u2019s sleek and strong as steel <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>teak wood cum rosewood ship and NOT in the slow lumbering and ponderous Chinese junk, which can be attacked by pirated if stand alone. </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-VFeeEFdjczA/TnsP9SiRtQI/AAAAAAAAGWA/v97Zhp1IkBU/s1600/images+%25288%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-VFeeEFdjczA/TnsP9SiRtQI/AAAAAAAAGWA/v97Zhp1IkBU/s1600/images+%25288%2529.jpg\" width=\"252\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">This is the reason why Chinese junks sailed as a fleet. It was NOT to show superiority in numbers. It was necessary for survival. Due to the slow pace of the huge junks having huge cargo holds, smaller ships had to accompany them to ward off pirates. Extra ships means extra food and water ships. </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-cTnq3Z0LfcQ/TnsQDoj00iI/AAAAAAAAGWE/I9lkEvLVZ8U/s1600/ZHENG_2_56604.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-cTnq3Z0LfcQ/TnsQDoj00iI/AAAAAAAAGWE/I9lkEvLVZ8U/s320/ZHENG_2_56604.jpg\" width=\"298\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Along with traders were usual sailors, soldiers, artists, doctors, teachers, explorers, historians, translators etc. Smaller patrol boats with 10 oars, doubling up as tugs, for clumsy Junks to enter river mouths <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>were also in this fleet. And imagine the water ships 130 feet long <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>held fresh water in tanks for 31000 people for two months.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-DfukSbFyRbo/TnsP5IMa-hI/AAAAAAAAGV8/vXLX9nTOoGc/s1600/download.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-DfukSbFyRbo/TnsP5IMa-hI/AAAAAAAAGV8/vXLX9nTOoGc/s1600/download.jpg\" width=\"201\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">The pepper sent from Calicut to China was in the regions of thousand of tonnes, and this huge dried up and powdered stock lasted for hundreds of years after China closed the bamboo doors to the world, after Zheng's death.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-jS3_x6CRcyA/TnsRx2QE9cI/AAAAAAAAGWk/hFffoKew6PI/s1600/e.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-jS3_x6CRcyA/TnsRx2QE9cI/AAAAAAAAGWk/hFffoKew6PI/s1600/e.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Even from Calicut record stating that his huge fleet sailed as one unit is NOT true. He split his fleet to conclude all operations on return passage in the Arabian sea by the end of May , prior to the start of the SW monsoon. </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-oS49M0GfFMA/TnsP02fwKUI/AAAAAAAAGV4/e-v-ValxbhA/s1600/download+%25284%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-oS49M0GfFMA/TnsP02fwKUI/AAAAAAAAGV4/e-v-ValxbhA/s1600/download+%25284%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Calicut was just a trade hub, for Zheng bartered in 34 countries en route including Persian Gulf, Red sea and East Africa. One of his faster junks was accompanied by the Calicut King's ship&nbsp;till Cape Verde\u2014which is where major part of Tripunka or Atlantis sank after being hit by Pashupatastra or the Scalar interferometer missile of Lord Shiva., as per lore.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-_EFSuG_MIQE/TnsRHvtnM-I/AAAAAAAAGWQ/w5lRUzSOc7c/s1600/images%252B%25252878%252529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-_EFSuG_MIQE/TnsRHvtnM-I/AAAAAAAAGWQ/w5lRUzSOc7c/s1600/images%252B%25252878%252529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">The Chinese fishing nets in Cochin were introduced by Zheng\u2019s great grandfather.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-YdqsJd76F4o/TnsPwXMjUiI/AAAAAAAAGV0/nha7_R14jvU/s1600/india_1.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"213\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-YdqsJd76F4o/TnsPwXMjUiI/AAAAAAAAGV0/nha7_R14jvU/s320/india_1.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">Zheng He\u2019s grave in China is empty. However it contains a lock of his hair and his sword with Islamic inscriptions \u201cAllahuakhbar \u201c.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-OODUIrBH22M/TnteXrFiucI/AAAAAAAAGXs/CnyVmpqa4e0/s1600/imagesbfr.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-OODUIrBH22M/TnteXrFiucI/AAAAAAAAGXs/CnyVmpqa4e0/s1600/imagesbfr.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">It was in Zheng He\u2019s time and as per his suggestion that the Chinese Capital was shifted to present day Beijing from Nanjing in 1421.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-vjx4g5oTjs8/TnteiNX2UdI/AAAAAAAAGXw/wD6dj7-BUys/s1600/imagescfy.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"219\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-vjx4g5oTjs8/TnteiNX2UdI/AAAAAAAAGXw/wD6dj7-BUys/s1600/imagescfy.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">With Admiral Zheng\u2019s death at Calicut in 1433, the world lost its greatest Admiral and a Genius and a great and imposing leader of men. His memorial grave in China has 7 steps--signifying 7 great voyages.</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-NAH8xtixrGc/TnsOZ8zl45I/AAAAAAAAGVM/-FuE3676dmQ/s1600/zhenghe%2527s+tomb.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-NAH8xtixrGc/TnsOZ8zl45I/AAAAAAAAGVM/-FuE3676dmQ/s1600/zhenghe%2527s+tomb.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">His stature on this planet can hardly be surpassed--yet how many people know about him?. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">Today you may wonder why there are NO Chinese and Jews in Calicut today. The Russian merchant arrived in India in 1469 and lived in the country for three years, travelling all the way to Kerala and Sri Lanka.<br />\n<br />\nFrom Dabhol, Nikitin traveled to Calicut in what was a 25-day journey --- \u201cCalicut is a big harbor on the Indian Sea, and God forbid that any ship should pass by it; no one who sails past it will cross the sea unscathed,\u201d he wrote. \u201cAnd it produces pepper, ginger, nutmeg, cinnamon, clove, spices, adrak, and many kinds of herbs. Athanasius (also known as Afanasy) Nikitin was in India nearly thirty years before Vasco da Gama and, in fact, opened the country for Europeans. After Nikitin, however, it took two centuries to establish direct contact between India and Russia. It was only in the late 17th century that Russian merchant Semyon Malenkiy brought a letter from Peter-the-Great to the Badshah, Mughal-Emperor-Aurangzeb, with a request to allow him to sell Russian goods, as well as purchase local products.
