text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://1.gvt0.com/vi/FI1AmTa-bV0/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/FI1AmTa-bV0&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/FI1AmTa-bV0&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-caj7gn0LAhw/TnsMAYJu8qI/AAAAAAAAGVA/UZvWd0Rr6q8/s1600/11082011413.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-caj7gn0LAhw/TnsMAYJu8qI/AAAAAAAAGVA/UZvWd0Rr6q8/s320/11082011413.jpg\" width=\"293\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 115%;\">..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "34", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/3053792148666990388/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "8946100332797594516", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2011-09-22T10:13:00+05:30", "updated": "2011-09-22T10:13:05+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMzE2NjY2NTg1ODU0Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2011/09/chlorinated-solvents-on-chemical.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/8946100332797594516", "title": "CHLORINATED SOLVENTS ON CHEMICAL TANKERS-  CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-8Z4stcshC-A/Tnq5e28PY4I/AAAAAAAAGU4/VtyBgTM45hI/s1600/xxc.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-8Z4stcshC-A/Tnq5e28PY4I/AAAAAAAAGU4/VtyBgTM45hI/s1600/xxc.png\" /></a></div><br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 16pt;\"><span style=\"font-size: x-large;\">CHLORINATED SOLVENTS</span> <o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><br />\n&nbsp;</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Chlorinated solvents are generally insoluble in water, and cleaning effect is limited to removing HC and other contaminants insoluble in water. They are hazardous to health. Carrying this cargo has a good cleaning effect on tank lining. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Chlorinated/ Brominated solvents hydrolyse in presence of water to form Organic and Inorganic acids which spoil the paint coating. &nbsp;Shippers must give the moisture content in PPM. Water content should not exceed 100 ppm or 0.01% especially for epoxy.&nbsp; Nitrogen pad is a must to exclude moisture.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Prior loading them take samples at manifold drain and line drain in brown narrow mouth self sealing sample bottles and also one clear bottle to check for clarity.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Chlorinated solvents must not be heated. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">They are heavier than water and sink to the bottom. So when taking samples when you load Chlor solvents look for water on the surface of the cargo in the bottle.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Examples of chlorinated solvents are Methylene Chloride , Carbon Tetra Chloride,&nbsp; Perchloroethylene , Trichloroethylene , Ethylene Di Chloride, Chloroform etc.&nbsp; Methylene Chloride is biodegradable under both aerobic and anaerobic conditions.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Neoprene and natural rubber gaskets swell. So use Teflon or Viton gaskets. Check paint resistance tables for compatibility and also restrictions for previous cargoes. Check cargo flexible hose resistance tables too. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Chlorinated solvents are not loaded after Styrene and other monomers, Acrylates, Latex, Fats, Fatty acids, Nitriles, Epoxy resins , DOP etc due to NVM.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">As a tank cleaning chemical, spraying of chlorinated solvents is not allowed.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Chlorinated HC does not by themselves attack SS. It is the impurities or decomposition products like Hydrogen chloride and Chlorides in the residual water phases which do the honours. If the products are acidic and contain high concentration of Chlorides, corrosion may occur.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Due to NVM Chlor solvents are not loaded after Monomers, Acrylates, Latex, Resins, Fatty acids, DOP, Nitriles , Palm oils, Fish oils , Glycols etc.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">RECIRC OF CHLORINATED SOLVENTS<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">First check if the chlorinated solvent is compatible with the coating and the last cargo. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">The Butterworth hose must be chemical resistant as the recirc is in full strength.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">When recirc tank with chlorinated solvents the tanks must be first to water-white standard and DRY ( except for Latex and Isocyanates like TDI/MDI ) or discoloration will take place with damage . </span><br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Chlorinated solvents have high evaporation factor . So keep PV valve shut while recirc. When recirc use a filter at the recirc flange or spider/ octopus. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">After recirc remove the solvent and steam tank thoroughly. &nbsp;Drain tank and vent dry. Then spray Methanol which dissolves any traces of Perchloroethylene . Hotwash tank for one hour . Tank is now ready.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Since chlorinated solvent and water form acid compounds which can adversely affect tank coating and since this mixture dilutes the cleaning capability of the Chlorinated solvent, water should never be added to any Chlorinated solvent.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Generally one drum of 200 litres of solvent is needed for 100 cum.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Get the specs of Chlorinated HC before loading\u2014 Chlorides, water and Hydrogen chloride content. Also check the SS resistance tables. Clean tanks immediately after dischg even if they are not to be loaded again soon.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"TxBrp3\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-left: 0in; tab-stops: 10.2pt 94.95pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-size: 11pt;\">Chlorinated solvents are slowly hydrolyzed to acids, normally this is not a problem except if tank cleaning is stopped in an early stage.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Water will make the chlorinated solvent recirculation less effective. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Effect is also less on hot bulkheads due to adjacent heat. Methylene chloride evaporates more than Trichloethylene and Perchloroethylene as its VP is very high and BP very less\u2014hence you require a large quantity of Methylene Chloride say\u201410 tons for an average sized tank. TCE evaporates the least. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">If you don\u2019t have Methanol on board, Graco inject light solution of Teepol in cold water and then wash off with hot water.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">TRICHLOROETHYLENE<o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">After dischg Isocyanate tanks have to be washed with non reactive solvent like chlorinated solvents and NEVER water. The urethane layer which forms will be very difficult to remove. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Chris code/ TCL<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">USCG/ 36<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Colourless watery liquid, chloroform type sweet odour<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Liquid on contact with very high temp/ flame&nbsp; can decompose to form phosgene which is highly toxic<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Non flammable , irritates eyes and skin<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Slowly decomposed by light in the presence of moisture to form HCL<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Suspected carcinogen<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Prolonged skin contact can cause dermatitis<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Sinks in water<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">SG/ 1.46<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">BP/ 87C<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">VD/ 4.5<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">VP/ 0.077 bars\u201480 mm hg at 20C<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">AH/ 38c<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">TLV/ 50 ppm<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">MARPOL category\u2014Y<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Not flammable<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Moisture sensitive and can become acidic when wet<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Excellent degreaser for extraction of oils/ fats and waxes<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Used in drycleaning, tanning industry , fumigant etc<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Not water soluble and hence requires emulsifier/ detergent <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Mixing with water weakens capability\u2014tank must be dry<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Must not be heated<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Spraying is not permitted<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Check resistance of tank cleaning hoses prior recirc <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">When recirc use filter at spider.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">After recirc vent and spray methanol to remove traces of solvent \u2013then hot wash <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Soluble in alchohol ethers and petroleum distillates<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"textcontent\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"color: black; font-size: 11pt; mso-ansi-language: EN;\">A very good solvent. Easily strips paints. Dissolves some plastics</span></div><div class=\"textcontent\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"color: black; font-size: 11pt; mso-ansi-language: EN;\">When inhaled, trichloroethylene as with any anesthetic gas, depresses the central nervous system. Its symptoms are similar to those of alcohol intoxication, beginning with headache, dizziness, and confusion and progressing with increasing exposure to unconsciousness.</span><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-size: 11pt;\"> </span><br />\n<br />\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-size: 11pt;\">Breathing large amounts of trichloroethylene may cause impaired heart function, unconsciousness, and death. Breathing it for long periods may cause nerve, kidney, and liver damage. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-size: 11pt;\">The International Agency for Research on Cancer (IARC) has determined that trichloroethylene is \u201cprobably carcinogenic to humans.\u201d </span><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"color: black; font-size: 11pt; mso-ansi-language: EN;\">California EPA regulators consider it a known carcinogen</span></div><div class=\"textcontent\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"color: black; font-size: 11pt;\">Trichloroethylene is noticeable by smell at approximately 82 ppm and above. However, people can become accustomed to the odour and may not smell it until higher concentrations are reached.</span><br />\n<br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">PERCHLOROETHYLENE:<o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">After dischg Isocyanate tanks have to be washed with non reactive solvent like chlorinated solvents and NEVER water. The urethane layer which forms will be very difficult to remove. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Before recirc remove all traces of water from tank<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">After recirc steam tank for 4 hours---drain tank vent<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Perchloroethylene is soluble in methanol<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">CAT/Y<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">VP/ 14.2 mm HG at 20c<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">VD/ 5.83<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">SG/ 1.625<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">BP/ 121C<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">AH/ 40C<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">TLV/ 50C<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Insoluble in water and requires the use of a emulsifier / detergent and then a solvent to remove from tank. Then warm wash.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Perchloroethylene, like most organic solvents, affects your brain the same way drinking alcohol does. Drinking alcohol within a few hours of exposure increases these effects, because the effects of perchloroethyelene and alcohol add together<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\"><br />\n</span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 11pt;\">If you are repeatedly overexposed for several days, you may be less affected as you develop a tolerance for overexposure. If a day or two then passes with no exposure, you may feel withdrawal symptoms such as nervousness, anxiety, and shakiness. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 11pt;\"><br />\n</span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 11pt;\">Perchloroethylene&nbsp; is a potential cancer-causing substance (carcinogen). <o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 11pt;\"><br />\n</span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 11pt;\">Exposure to a carcinogen does not necessarily mean that you will get cancer. In general, the greater the exposure, the greater the risk of developing cancer. The best way to protect your health is to keep your exposure as low as possible. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-size: 11pt;\"><br />\n</span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"color: black; font-size: 11pt; mso-ansi-language: EN;\">Use it for its solvent properties. Most organic materials dissolve in perchloroethylene. It is the most widely used solvent in drycleaning and for degreasing,&nbsp; including paint strippers and spot removers.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN\" style=\"color: black; font-size: 11pt; mso-ansi-language: EN;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Instead or recirc with Diesel oil, in this strict prewash Marpol age , Perchloroethylene can be used.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">METHYLENE CHLORIDE<o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">After dischg Isocyanate tanks have to be washed with non reactive solvent like chlorinated solvents and NEVER water. The urethane layer which forms will be very difficult to remove. Instead or recirc with DO , Dichloromethane or Methylene chloride can be used.</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif; font-size: 15px;\">&nbsp;</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; font-size: 11pt;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">Highly volatile<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11pt;\">Attacks plastics<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: 10.2pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: black;  </span></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 14.25pt; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"background: rgb(238, 238, 204); font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Don\u2019t rely on past practice ( of old timers ) , to find out if Paraffin wax requires a pre-wash ashore after discharge .</span><span style=\"background: rgb(238, 238, 204); text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"background: yellow; font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">As you know since 1<span style=\"font-size: small;\"><sup>st</sup>&nbsp;Jan 2007\u2014the Marpol prewash rules for high viscosity oils have changed. It is better to get the unloading temperature and the viscosity of Paraffin Wax at that temperature declared in writing in a proper signed and sealed document .</span></span><span style=\"background: rgb(238, 238, 204); font-family: &quot;Trebuchet MS&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 14.25pt; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 14.25pt; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"background: rgb(238, 238, 204); font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Ideally the viscocity in mPas at 20 deg C should be declared in the B/ lading \u2014as this figure may vary or may be deliberately fudged.</span><span style=\"background: rgb(238, 238, 204); font-family: &quot;Trebuchet MS&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Cleaning is more or less the same for all grades of paraffin wax, the only difference is the amount of residues remaining in tank - wax on the coils and under frames and the amount of white hard powder residue on bulkheads and floors. </span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Melting Points of<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>waxes differ greatly from different load ports and so the MP and heating instructions must be obtained in writing. You may do your own melting point test of a composite sample in the ships lab. Don\u2019t allow steam inside the coils to scorch the cargo, form a insulation coating and lose heating capacity.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">At the loadport remove all adjacent cold interface from SBT.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count: 2;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Once the steam coils are covered during loading, you should start slow heating in the tank .<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count: 2;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The importance of repeatedly checking PV valve and lines during cold weather and bad weather for blockage by wax during the voyage cannot be over-emphasised. This may have to be checked physically by opening tank hatch and remove solidified wax from vent line.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Before arrival at the discharging port, open the tank dome and one of the butterworth ports to check for solid cargo build up. Quite often after a freezing bad weather passage you may find that the huge orifice ( like tank dome or butterworth port ) is reduced to 20%. Run the framo pump to check if the impellers are free .<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n&nbsp;</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Check if the delivery lines are clear\u2014it is common place to have them fully blocked. If it is not 100% blocked it must be understood that the hot cargo will scour and clear the lines 100% when it flows through. Use hot steaming water to melt wax internally inside valves by wrapping soaker rags \u2013live steam is too local and unwieldy / thermally ineffective. Live steam is too local and takes too long to melt wax. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n&nbsp;</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Samples at can be drawn from open tank domes\u2014it is usual for the UTI sampler to get stuck in the extension tube.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Wax tanks should be discharged separately, one by one\u2014don\u2019t use the common collector. Steam tracing the common collector at manifold is also not the best way out.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Do not let shore personnel put pressure on the ship to rig more than one by one unless they supply separate shore hose. Make sure you make a protest letter to cover you up in case there are delays due to frozen lines.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  <span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">During discharge, if have to stop pumping for any reason, steam line back to tank immediately to avoid blocked lines. In the pre-loading meeting find out if there are any stoppages due to shore reason and be stand by with steam hoses in hold weather.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Heating coils should be tuned down just before bottom coils are uncovered<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  <span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">When ballasting avoid frozen wax on tank sides and bottom. Chief officer must personally ensure there is no cold interface.</span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n&nbsp;</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">Cleaning;</span> <o:p></o:p></span></span></i></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">First steam the tank for one hour after removing adjacent ballast. Place extra cleaning machines in tank by hanging off at tank dome too. Let the hot sea water flow from tankcleaning line till the temp at tank inlet is 80C. Machine drops should be maximum 2.5 m, one hour each, temperature at outlet of tank cleaning heater should be 90<span style=\"font-size: small;\"><sup>o</sup>C which will give approximately 80<sup>o</sup>C inside tank at full pressure. Don\u2019t compromise on both temp and pressure.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span></span></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">If it is absolutely necessary to compromise on either temperature or pressure, then it is better to slightly reduce the pressure ( not too much ) and maintain the correct temperature. Keep a continious written record of the temp at tankcleaning inlet say every 20 minutes. This wont be wasted manhours as the wax has to be melted first before being washed away. </span></span><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Clean with SW for 30 minutes hot, leave water in tank and keep steam coil heating on. Until discharging of the accumulated wash water keep live steam slowly into tank.</span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">After the initial hot salt water wash graco inject an emulsifier plus surfactant and continue the same way as before with short drops.</span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">In very cold weather only a chlorinated solvent ( Perchloroethylene or Trichloroethylene ) recirc can do the trick.</span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">At the end of your tankcleaning \u2013on tank man entry you may find hard white residue especially on heating coils \u2013the amount depending on the wax--which has to be removed manually. Dry up the coils by passing steam and use scotch brite and wood hammers to shake it off. Keep aluminium ladders standby to remove any NVM traces from bulkheads </span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">In stainless tanks, recirculate 40% metal brightener / 60% fresh water, approximately 3 cum at<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>45<span style=\"font-size: small;\"><sup>o</sup>C for 1.5 hours and then transfer to next tank. Finally rinse with hot fresh water for 30 min and steam tank.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>This is the final polish up act if the next cargo is WWT with UV test. </span></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: small;\">Caustic recirc at 4% can prepare epoxy tanks for the UV test.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Zinc tanks hence are unsuitable for Paraffin wax as you can see the pH of the recirculation solution is incompatible.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-7ss4cYCalDY/TnmS1cF95kI/AAAAAAAAGUk/eHou5MkrfgQ/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil+5.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "2", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/2750191460493907386/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "7559558743039580643", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2011-09-21T11:28:00+05:30", "updated": "2014-09-16T16:45:56+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxNDEwODY2MTU2MTE5Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2011/09/parrot-jokes-capt-ajit-vadakayil.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/7559558743039580643", "title": "PARROT JOKES -- CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-zTwKzFsv-zU/Tnl6r5KQHnI/AAAAAAAAGT0/hn9wSUyyi6I/s1600/untitled.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-zTwKzFsv-zU/Tnl6r5KQHnI/AAAAAAAAGT0/hn9wSUyyi6I/s1600/untitled.png\" height=\"320\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\nOld legendary pirates kept parrots as pets. In addition to being early warning radars, they provided them amusement too.<br />\n<br />\nI know of a Jack fruit ( Chakka trader ) shopkeeper who trained his parrot to say in Malalayam \" Dont give the good jackfruit, give him the bad one kept in that corner\".&nbsp; He did roaring business, as customers found this hilarious.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nLet me put&nbsp;down some spicy parrot jokes.&nbsp; <span style=\"color: blue; font-size: x-large;\">enjoy!</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://0.gvt0.com/vi/K7ht0a2-OnA/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/K7ht0a2-OnA&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/K7ht0a2-OnA&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Ho-7EJIwYo0/Tnl6m9qxaMI/AAAAAAAAGTw/X2lkXf-3faY/s1600/imagesCAB6MWFX.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Ho-7EJIwYo0/Tnl6m9qxaMI/AAAAAAAAGTw/X2lkXf-3faY/s1600/imagesCAB6MWFX.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: x-large;\">MONICA:</span><br />\n<br />\nMonica Lewisnky had a parrot whose previous owner was a whore in a brothel. The parrot would give running commentary , as soon as the act on bed started . <br />\n<br />\nBeing intelligent the conscious parrot gave unique punch lines , appropriate to the scenario. Examples-<br />\n<br />\nHERE COMES THE GUN OF NAVARONE--<br />\nWALL IS DOWN, PINK FLOYD IS NOW PEEPIN' OUT--<br />\nSECURITY BREACH NOW, AT LOS PANTALONES--<br />\nTHIS SOLDIER AIN'T UNKNOWN AT ALL --<br />\nPOPEYE GETTING SOME SHORE LEAVE NOW --<br />\nOUR NEXT GUEST NEEDS NO INTRODUCTION--<br />\nPAGING MR JOHNSON, PAGING MR JOHNSON--<br />\n<br />\nBill Clinton&nbsp;had heard about this parrot and asked&nbsp;Monica to bring the parrot to the White house . As soon as Bill unzips, Hillary walks into Oval office unannounced. <br />\n<br />\nBill zips up immediately and pretends to work, while Monica ducks deep under the presidential desk .<br />\n<br />\nThe parrot hung at the corner now screams her head off \" <span style=\"font-size: large;\">FLY SHIFTED BACK FROM MONICA&nbsp;TO HILLARY MODE , JUST NOW !</span>\"<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-W3Htf6gOMd4/Tnl6wMCeEVI/AAAAAAAAGT4/SoH_Qu4r-kc/s1600/imagesCA8GOM6E.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-W3Htf6gOMd4/Tnl6wMCeEVI/AAAAAAAAGT4/SoH_Qu4r-kc/s1600/imagesCA8GOM6E.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: x-large;\">SITTING ON A SUITCASE</span>:<br />\n<br />\nA couple was about to leave for their honeymoon. <br />\n<br />\nThe woman wants to take her parrot along. The man was not so keen as the parrot was raised in a brothel. <br />\n<br />\nHowever the woman has her way , when she promised that the cage would be covered with a black cloth all the time. <br />\n<br />\nThey check&nbsp;into a hotel at a&nbsp;distant holiday resort. They get into bed. <br />\n<br />\nSoon the woman remembers that in the heat of their&nbsp;argument, she had forgotten to lock the front door, and the key was still on the door, in a bad neighbourhood. <br />\n<br />\nSo they decide to rush back. They pack up the suitcase, but the lid wont shut as they had done some shopping in town. <br />\n<br />\nSo the man said \" Let me sit on it \" and sat&nbsp;on the suitcase cover, but it was not possible to lock the suitcase. <br />\n<br />\nThen woman said \" You get up, let me sit on it!\". The suitcase still would not shut.<br />\n<br />\nSo the man said \" Shift a little , let us both sit on it!\". <br />\n<br />\nImmediately the parrot jumps up and down in the cage , screams her head off from behind the black cloth \" <span style=\"font-size: large;\">THIS I WANNA SEE--THIS I WANNA SEE--</span>&nbsp;!\"<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-b00r_cMbZxA/Tnl60-xWkCI/AAAAAAAAGT8/8h6FRMuYBkw/s1600/imagesCAGA1W06.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-b00r_cMbZxA/Tnl60-xWkCI/AAAAAAAAGT8/8h6FRMuYBkw/s1600/imagesCAGA1W06.jpg\" height=\"240\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: x-large;\">SEX EDUCATION CLASS</span> :<br />\n<br />\nA 13 year old girl takes her pet&nbsp;parrot to school. She has exams and as soon as the test was over she planned to&nbsp;visit her grandparents, direct from school.<br />\n<br />\nThe exams were a ploy, instead a sex education class started. The teacher went on and on about the birds and the bees--<br />\n<br />\nAfter some time the parrot screams from inside the school bag \" <span style=\"font-size: large;\">ALL THOSE WHO KNOW FUCKIN' --CAN THEY GO HOME </span>?\"<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; font-size: x-large;\">CAPTAIN'S PARROT:</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\">A magician was working on a luxury cruise ship in the Caribbean. </span></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\"></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\">The audience would be different each week, so the magician allowed himself to do the same tricks over and over again. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\">There was only one problem: The captain's parrot saw the shows each week and began to understand how the magician did his&nbsp;tricks.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\">So she would upset the show by revealing the secrets&nbsp;-- </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\">\"Look, it&nbsp;ain't the same hat\" </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\">\"Look, he is hiding the balls under the table\" </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\">\"Hey, why are all the cards the Ace of Hearts ?\" </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\">The magician was furious but couldn't do anything; it was, after all, the captain's parrot, and his job was well paying. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\">One day the ship had a collision&nbsp;and sank. The magician found himself on a piece of wood in the middle of the ocean with the parrot, for sole company. They eyeballed each other for a while , and then decided to ignore each other. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\">This went on for a day and then another and another. </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\">After a week the parrot screams&nbsp; : \"<span style=\"font-size: large;\">OK, I give up. Calibri;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\">He pulled on the&nbsp;left string, and the parrot sang a melodious \"Jingle Bells\". </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" Silent nights\". </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\">Then woman asked 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: x-large;\">BOSS MAN:</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\">A man goes into a pet shop to buy a parrot. </span></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\"></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\">The shop owner points to 3 identical looking parrots on a perch and says: \"The parrot on the left costs a thousand dollars\". </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\">\"Why does that one cost so much?\" asked the shopper. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\">The owner says \"Well the parrot is computer savvy\" </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\">The man then asks about the next parrot and was told that this one costs two thousand dollars&nbsp;, because it can do everything the other parrot can do plus it knows the UNIX operating system. </span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\"><br />\nThe&nbsp;curious man asks about the third parrot to be told that it costs one million dollars. </span><span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\"></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\"></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Calibri;\"></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\"
